&lt;div class=&quot;CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;CodeTabs-toolbar&quot; role=&quot;tablist&quot;&gt;&lt;button aria-selected=&quot;true&quot; class=&quot;CodeTabs_active&quot; role=&quot;tab&quot; type=&quot;button&quot;&gt;YAML&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;CodeTabs-inner&quot; role=&quot;tabpanel&quot;&gt;&lt;pre&gt;&lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;yaml&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;apiVersion: external-secrets.io/v1
kind: SecretStore
metadata:
  name: akeyless-store
  namespace: app-test
spec:
  provider:
    akeyless:
      akeylessGWApiURL: &amp;quot;https://api.akeyless.io&amp;quot;
      # Optional: use a specific ServiceAccount for ESO controller in this namespace
      serviceAccountRef:
        name: app-test
      authSecretRef:
        secretRef:
          accessID:
            name: akeyless-azure-creds
            key: accessId
          accessType:
            name: akeyless-azure-creds
            key: accessType
          accessTypeParam:
            name: akeyless-azure-creds
            key: accessTypeParam
&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/pre&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;h4 class=&quot;heading heading-4 header-scroll&quot; align=&quot;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-anchor anchor waypoint&quot; id=&quot;externalsecret-consuming-a-secret-by-way-of-the-secretstore&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-text&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;section-external-secret-consuming-a-secret-by-way-of-the-secret-store&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;ExternalSecret Consuming a Secret by way of the SecretStore&lt;/div&gt;&lt;a aria-label=&quot;Skip link to ExternalSecret Consuming a Secret by way of the SecretStore&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor&quot; href=&quot;#externalsecret-consuming-a-secret-by-way-of-the-secretstore&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;CodeTabs-toolbar&quot; role=&quot;tablist&quot;&gt;&lt;button aria-selected=&quot;true&quot; class=&quot;CodeTabs_active&quot; role=&quot;tab&quot; type=&quot;button&quot;&gt;YAML&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;CodeTabs-inner&quot; role=&quot;tabpanel&quot;&gt;&lt;pre&gt;&lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;yaml&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;apiVersion: external-secrets.io/v1
kind: ExternalSecret
metadata:
  name: app-api-secret
  namespace: app-test
spec:
  refreshInterval: 1h
  secretStoreRef:
    name: akeyless-store
    kind: SecretStore
  target:
    name: app-api-secret
    creationPolicy: Owner
  data:
    - secretKey: api-key
      remoteRef:
        key: /devops/static_secret_1
&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/pre&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;h4 class=&quot;heading heading-4 header-scroll&quot; align=&quot;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-anchor anchor waypoint&quot; id=&quot;retrieving-the-synced-secret&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-text&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;section-retrieving-the-synced-secret&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;Retrieving the Synced Secret&lt;/div&gt;&lt;a aria-label=&quot;Skip link to Retrieving the Synced Secret&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor&quot; href=&quot;#retrieving-the-synced-secret&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;
&lt;div class=&quot;CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;CodeTabs-toolbar&quot; role=&quot;tablist&quot;&gt;&lt;button aria-selected=&quot;true&quot; class=&quot;CodeTabs_active&quot; role=&quot;tab&quot; type=&quot;button&quot;&gt;Shell&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;CodeTabs-inner&quot; role=&quot;tabpanel&quot;&gt;&lt;pre&gt;&lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang-shell theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;shell&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;kubectl -n app-test get secret app-api-secret -o jsonpath=&amp;quot;{.data.api-key}&amp;quot; | base64 -d
&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/pre&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;p&gt;This pattern ties together:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;AKS nodes or workloads using &lt;strong&gt;Managed Identity&lt;/strong&gt;,&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;An Akeyless &lt;strong&gt;Azure AD Auth Method&lt;/strong&gt; with sub-claim constraints, and&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;ESO as the consumer that syncs secrets into Kubernetes.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;hr/&gt;
&lt;h2 class=&quot;heading heading-2 header-scroll&quot; align=&quot;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-anchor anchor waypoint&quot; id=&quot;tutorial&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-text&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;section-tutorial&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;Tutorial&lt;/div&gt;&lt;a aria-label=&quot;Skip link to Tutorial&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor&quot; href=&quot;#tutorial&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;p&gt;For a hands-on walkthrough, check out our tutorial video on &lt;a href=&quot;https://tutorials.akeyless.io/docs/sync-secrets-to-k8s-with-external-secrets-operator&quot; target=&quot;&quot; title=&quot;&quot;&gt;Sync Secrets to Kubernetes with External Secrets Operator (ESO)&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;" style="margin-left:31px" class="rm-Markdown markdown-body rm-Markdown markdown-body ng-non-bindable" data-testid="RDMD"><p>This guide shows how to integrate the <strong>Akeyless Platform</strong> with the <strong><a target="_self" href="https://external-secrets.io/latest/provider/akeyless/">External Secrets Operator (ESO)</a></strong> to synchronize secrets between Akeyless and Kubernetes.</p>
<p>It covers:</p>
<ul>
<li>Installing ESO with Helm</li>
<li>Configuring authentication from Kubernetes to Akeyless (API Key, Kubernetes Auth, Azure AD, and other cloud identities)</li>
<li>Using <a target="_self" href="https://external-secrets.io/latest/api/secretstore/">SecretStore</a>, <a target="_self" href="https://external-secrets.io/latest/api/clustersecretstore/">ClusterSecretStore</a>, and <a target="_self" href="https://external-secrets.io/latest/api/externalsecret/">ExternalSecret</a> to fetch secrets</li>
<li>Using <a target="_self" href="https://external-secrets.io/latest/api/pushsecret/">PushSecret</a> to push Kubernetes secrets back to Akeyless</li>
<li>Example usage</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="how-eso-works-with-akeyless"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-how-eso-works-with-akeyless" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>How ESO Works With Akeyless</div><a aria-label="Skip link to How ESO Works With Akeyless" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#how-eso-works-with-akeyless"></a></h2>
<p>The <strong>External Secrets Operator</strong> is a Kubernetes operator that reads secrets from external systems (such as Akeyless) and creates or updates <a target="_self" href="https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/configuration/secret/">standard Kubernetes Secret objects</a> in a Kubernetes cluster.</p>
<p>For Akeyless, ESO uses the following custom resources:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">SecretStore</code></strong>: namespaced definition of how to connect and authenticate to Akeyless.</li>
<li><strong><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ClusterSecretStore</code></strong>: cluster-wide variant of <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">SecretStore</code>.</li>
<li><strong><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ExternalSecret</code></strong>: defines which Akeyless items to sync into which Kubernetes Secret object.</li>
<li><strong><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">PushSecret</code></strong>: pushes a Kubernetes Secret from the cluster into Akeyless.</li>
</ul>
<p>At a high level:</p>
<ol>
<li>ESO authenticates to Akeyless using the method specified in <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">SecretStore</code> or <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ClusterSecretStore</code>.</li>
<li>ESO fetches secrets from Akeyless.</li>
<li>ESO writes those values into Kubernetes Secrets (or pushes them back to Akeyless in the case of <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">PushSecret</code>).</li>
<li>ESO periodically refreshes secrets according to the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">refreshInterval</code> on each <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ExternalSecret</code> or <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">PushSecret</code>.</li>
</ol>
<p><span aria-label="Illustration for: 3. ESO writes those values into Kubernetes Secrets (or pushes them back to Akeyless in the case of PushSecret). 4. ESO periodically refreshes secrets according to the…" class="img lightbox closed" role="button" tabindex="0"><span class="lightbox-inner"><img alt="Illustration for: 3. ESO writes those values into Kubernetes Secrets (or pushes them back to Akeyless in the case of PushSecret). 4. ESO periodically refreshes secrets according to the…" loading="lazy" src="https://files.readme.io/143d329a383df21e1e4481289a4d1be018652093b525d21d77e2b6d758efa807-External_Secrets_Operator_1.jpg" align="" caption="" height="auto" title="" width="auto"/></span></span></p>
<hr/>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="architecture--resources"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-architecture-resources" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Architecture &amp; Resources</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Architecture &amp; Resources" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#architecture--resources"></a></h2>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="in-cluster-components"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-in-cluster-components" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>In-Cluster Components</div><a aria-label="Skip link to In-Cluster Components" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#in-cluster-components"></a></h3>
<ul>
<li>The ESO controller runs as a Kubernetes <strong>Deployment</strong>.</li>
<li>It watches custom resources: <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ExternalSecret</code>, <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">SecretStore</code>, <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ClusterSecretStore</code>, and <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">PushSecret</code>.</li>
<li>It reconciles the desired state by calling Akeyless APIs to create and update Kubernetes Secret objects.</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="akeyless-side"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-akeyless-side" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Akeyless Side</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Akeyless Side" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#akeyless-side"></a></h3>
<ul>
<li>Akeyless <strong>Authentication Methods</strong> define how Kubernetes workloads authenticate (For example, API Key, Kubernetes Auth, Azure AD, AWS IAM, GCP).</li>
<li><strong>Access Roles</strong> control which Akeyless items (paths) a given authentication identity may access.</li>
<li>ESO uses an <strong>Access ID</strong> (and additional auth parameters) to obtain a token and read or write secrets.</li>
</ul>
<hr/>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="prerequisites"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-prerequisites" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Prerequisites</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Prerequisites" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#prerequisites"></a></h2>
<ul>
<li>A running Kubernetes cluster, <strong>v1.16+</strong> (ESO requirement).</li>
<li><strong>Helm</strong> installed locally.</li>
<li>An Akeyless tenant with:
<ul>
<li>At least one <strong>Authentication Method</strong> (API Key, Kubernetes Auth, Azure AD, AWS IAM, or GCP).</li>
<li>An <strong>Access Role</strong> that grants read or write permissions to the relevant secrets.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>For Kubernetes Auth, private deployments, or hybrid deployments:
<ul>
<li>An <strong>Akeyless Gateway</strong> with network access to the Kubernetes API server.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<hr/>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="installing-external-secrets-operator-with-helm"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-installing-external-secrets-operator-with-helm" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Installing External Secrets Operator With Helm</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Installing External Secrets Operator With Helm" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#installing-external-secrets-operator-with-helm"></a></h2>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Add the official ESO Helm repository:</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">Shell</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-shell theme-light" data-lang="shell" name="" tabindex="0">helm repo add external-secrets https://charts.external-secrets.io
helm repo update
</code></pre></div></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Install ESO (default configuration):</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">Shell</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-shell theme-light" data-lang="shell" name="" tabindex="0">helm install external-secrets external-secrets/external-secrets --namespace external-secrets --create-namespace
</code></pre></div></div>
</li>
</ol>
<p>The ESO controller pods running in the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">external-secrets</code> Namespace should now be running.</p>
<hr/>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="authentication-with-akeyless"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-authentication-with-akeyless" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Authentication With Akeyless</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Authentication With Akeyless" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#authentication-with-akeyless"></a></h2>
<p>ESO’s Akeyless provider supports the following <strong>access types</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">api_key</code></li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">k8s</code></li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">azure_ad</code></li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">aws_iam</code></li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">gcp</code></li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="callout callout_info" theme="ℹ️"><h2 class="callout-heading"><span class="callout-icon">ℹ️</span><p><strong>Note:</strong> For AKS Workload Identity, use the Azure AD Authentication Method (<button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">accessType: azure_ad</code>).</p></h2><p>When using <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">accessType: azure_ad</code>, ESO relies on the identity of the Kubernetes <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ServiceAccount</code> that runs the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ExternalSecret</code>. Identity is not selected through the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">SecretStore</code>. For full guidance, see (<a target="_self" href="/docs/eso-and-aks-workload-identity">https://docs.akeyless.io/docs/eso-and-aks-workload-identity</a>).</p><p>⚠️ <strong>Warning:</strong> OIDC is not supported as an <strong>access type</strong> at this time.</p></blockquote>
<p>Each Authentication Method in Akeyless exposes an <strong>Access ID</strong>, and for some methods, an additional parameter (<button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">accessTypeParam</code>) such as:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>API Key</strong> → <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">accessTypeParam</code>: Akeyless Access Key</li>
<li><strong>Kubernetes Auth</strong> → <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">accessTypeParam</code>: Kubernetes Auth config name</li>
<li><strong>Azure AD</strong> → <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">accessTypeParam</code>: Azure Object ID (optional)
<ul>
<li>See <a target="_self" href="/docs/eso-and-aks-workload-identity">ESO and AKS Workload Identity</a> for more information.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>GCP</strong> → <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">accessTypeParam</code>: GCP audience</li>
<li><strong>AWS IAM</strong> → <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">accessTypeParam</code>: not required</li>
</ul>
<p>ESO can authenticate in one of two ways:</p>
<ol>
<li>Using a <strong>credentials Secret</strong> (generic pattern, works for all supported access types).</li>
<li>Using <strong>Kubernetes Auth-specific fields</strong> (directly referencing a Kubernetes ServiceAccount and/or JWT).</li>
</ol>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="creating-a-credentials-secret"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-creating-a-credentials-secret" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Creating a Credentials Secret</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Creating a Credentials Secret" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#creating-a-credentials-secret"></a></h3>
<p>Store the Akeyless credentials that ESO should use within a Kubernetes Secret:</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">apiVersion: v1
kind: Secret
metadata:
  name: akeyless-secret-creds
  namespace: akeyless-demo
type: Opaque
stringData:
  accessId: &quot;p-XXXX&quot;                 # Access ID of the Akeyless Auth Method
  accessType: &quot;api_key&quot;              # api_key / k8s / azure_ad / aws_iam / gcp
  accessTypeParam: &quot;&lt;access-key&gt;&quot;
</code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="heading heading-4 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="api-key-example-not-recommended-for-production"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-api-key-example-not-recommended-for-production" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>API Key Example (NOT Recommended for Production)</div><a aria-label="Skip link to API Key Example (NOT Recommended for Production)" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#api-key-example-not-recommended-for-production"></a></h4>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">apiVersion: v1
kind: Secret
metadata:
  name: akeyless-api-creds
  namespace: akeyless-demo
type: Opaque
stringData:
  accessId: &quot;&lt;p-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx&gt;&quot;
  accessType: &quot;api_key&quot;
  accessTypeParam: &quot;&lt;YOUR-ACCESS-KEY-HERE&gt;&quot;
</code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="heading heading-4 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="kubernetes-auth-example"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-kubernetes-auth-example" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Kubernetes Auth Example</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Kubernetes Auth Example" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#kubernetes-auth-example"></a></h4>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">apiVersion: v1
kind: Secret
metadata:
  name: akeyless-k8s-creds
  namespace: akeyless-demo
type: Opaque
stringData:
  accessId: &quot;&lt;p-k8saccessid&gt;&quot;
  accessType: &quot;k8s&quot;
  accessTypeParam: &quot;&lt;my-k8s-auth-config-name&gt;&quot;
</code></pre></div></div>
<ul>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">accessId</code>: Access ID for the <strong>Kubernetes Auth</strong> method.</li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">accessTypeParam</code>: Name of the Kubernetes Auth config for the cluster.</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="heading heading-4 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="azure-ad-example-managed-identity-or-service-principal"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-azure-ad-example-managed-identity-or-service-principal" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Azure AD Example (Managed Identity or Service Principal)</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Azure AD Example (Managed Identity or Service Principal)" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#azure-ad-example-managed-identity-or-service-principal"></a></h4>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">apiVersion: v1
kind: Secret
metadata:
  name: akeyless-azure-creds
  namespace: akeyless-demo
type: Opaque
stringData:
  accessId: &quot;&lt;p-xxxxx&gt;&quot;
  accessType: &quot;azure_ad&quot;
  accessTypeParam: &quot;&quot;              # Optional: Azure Object ID; can be left empty if using sub-claims such as xms_mirid
</code></pre></div></div>
<p>This Secret is suitable when using Azure AD Managed Identity with sub-claim enforcement.</p>
<blockquote class="callout callout_info" theme="ℹ️"><h2 class="callout-heading"><span class="callout-icon">ℹ️</span><p><strong>Note:</strong> ESO does not implement Azure Workload Identity flows internally. When <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">accessType: azure_ad</code> is used, ESO relies entirely on the Azure AD token available in the pod’s environment. This is typically projected by way of AKS Workload Identity. Therefore, the identity ESO uses depends on the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ServiceAccount</code> the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ExternalSecret</code> runs under, not on the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">SecretStore</code>.</p></h2></blockquote>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="secretstore-namespaced-secret-provider"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-secret-store-namespaced-secret-provider" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">SecretStore</code>: Namespaced Secret Provider</div><a aria-label="Skip link to [object Object]" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#secretstore-namespaced-secret-provider"></a></h3>
<h4 class="heading heading-4 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="secretstore-using-a-credentials-secret"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-secret-store-using-a-credentials-secret" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">SecretStore</code> (Using a Credentials Secret)</div><a aria-label="Skip link to [object Object]" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#secretstore-using-a-credentials-secret"></a></h4>
<p>Create a <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">SecretStore</code> resource which defines how ESO connects to Akeyless within a single Namespace.</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">apiVersion: external-secrets.io/v1
kind: SecretStore
metadata:
  name: akeyless-secret-store
  namespace: akeyless-demo
spec:
  provider:
    akeyless:
      # Public SaaS API
      akeylessGWApiURL: &quot;https://api.akeyless.io&quot;
      authSecretRef:
        secretRef:
          accessID:
            name: akeyless-secret-creds
            key: accessId
          accessType:
            name: akeyless-secret-creds
            key: accessType
          accessTypeParam:
            name: akeyless-secret-creds
            key: accessTypeParam
</code></pre></div></div>
<p>If using a <strong>private Akeyless Gateway</strong> (for example in a zero-knowledge or hybrid deployment), set:</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">      akeylessGWApiURL: &quot;https://&lt;the.akeyless.gw&gt;:8000/api/v2&quot;
</code></pre></div></div>
<p>Custom CAs can be configured by way of <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">caBundle</code> or <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">caProvider</code> if the Akeyless Gateway uses a private CA.</p>
<h4 class="heading heading-4 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="secretstore-direct-kubernetes-auth"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-secret-store-direct-kubernetes-auth" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">SecretStore</code> (Direct Kubernetes Auth)</div><a aria-label="Skip link to [object Object]" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#secretstore-direct-kubernetes-auth"></a></h4>
<p>Alternatively, Kubernetes Auth can be configured directly in the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">SecretStore</code> without a generic credentials Secret.</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">apiVersion: external-secrets.io/v1
kind: SecretStore
metadata:
  name: akeyless-k8s-secret-store
  namespace: akeyless-demo
spec:
  provider:
    akeyless:
      akeylessGWApiURL: &quot;https://api.akeyless.io&quot;
      authSecretRef:
        kubernetesAuth:
          accessID: &quot;p-k8saccessid&quot;
          k8sConfName: &quot;my-k8s-auth-config-name&quot;
          serviceAccountRef:
            name: &quot;akeyless-demo-sa&quot;
          # Optional: Use a specific Secret containing a ServiceAccount JWT
          secretRef:
            name: &quot;akeyless-demo-sa-token&quot;
            key: &quot;token&quot;
</code></pre></div></div>
<h5 class="heading heading-5 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="key-fields"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-key-fields" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Key Fields</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Key Fields" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#key-fields"></a></h5>
<ul>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">accessID</code>: Access ID of the Kubernetes Auth Method.</li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">k8sConfName</code>: Kubernetes Auth config name attached to the cluster.</li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">serviceAccountRef</code>: <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ServiceAccount</code> that ESO uses to request and project tokens.</li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">secretRef</code>: Optional; explicit Secret containing a SA token ESO should use.</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="clustersecretstore-cluster-wide-secret-provider"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-cluster-secret-store-cluster-wide-secret-provider" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ClusterSecretStore</code>: Cluster-Wide Secret Provider</div><a aria-label="Skip link to [object Object]" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#clustersecretstore-cluster-wide-secret-provider"></a></h3>
<p>A <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ClusterSecretStore</code> is a cluster-scoped provider configuration that can be used by <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ExternalSecret</code> resources in any Namespace.</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">apiVersion: external-secrets.io/v1
kind: ClusterSecretStore
metadata:
  name: akeyless-cluster-secret-store
spec:
  provider:
    akeyless:
      akeylessGWApiURL: &quot;https://api.akeyless.io&quot;
      authSecretRef:
        secretRef:
          accessID:
            name: akeyless-secret-creds
            key: accessId
            namespace: akeyless-demo
          accessType:
            name: akeyless-secret-creds
            key: accessType
            namespace: akeyless-demo
          accessTypeParam:
            name: akeyless-secret-creds
            key: accessTypeParam
            namespace: akeyless-demo
</code></pre></div></div>
<p>For a <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ClusterSecretStore</code> object, the Namespace fields are required for <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">secretRef.accessID</code>, <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">secretRef.accessType</code>, and <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">secretRef.accessTypeParam</code> (and for any <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">serviceAccountRef</code> or <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">secretRef</code> when using the Kubernetes authentication method).</p>
<p>When using <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ClusterSecretStore</code>, the referencing <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ExternalSecret</code> must set <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">secretStoreRef</code> to use the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ClusterSecretStore</code> as opposed to a <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">SecretStore</code>:</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">secretStoreRef:
  kind: ClusterSecretStore
  name: akeyless-cluster-secret-store
</code></pre></div></div>
<p>Remember that any Namespace using this <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ClusterSecretStore</code> must be authorized in the Akeyless Platform with appropriate roles and claims.</p>
<hr/>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="externalsecret-syncing-akeyless-secrets-into-kubernetes"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-external-secret-syncing-akeyless-secrets-into-kubernetes" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ExternalSecret</code>: Syncing Akeyless Secrets Into Kubernetes</div><a aria-label="Skip link to [object Object]" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#externalsecret-syncing-akeyless-secrets-into-kubernetes"></a></h2>
<p>To fetch an Akeyless secret and store it as a Kubernetes Secret, define an <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ExternalSecret</code> resource.</p>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="basic-externalsecret-single-values"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-basic-external-secret-single-values" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Basic <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ExternalSecret</code> (Single Values)</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Basic " class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#basic-externalsecret-single-values"></a></h3>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">apiVersion: external-secrets.io/v1
kind: ExternalSecret
metadata:
  name: akeyless-external-secret
  namespace: akeyless-demo
spec:
  refreshInterval: 1h

  secretStoreRef:
    kind: SecretStore
    name: akeyless-secret-store

  target:
    name: app-config-secret
    creationPolicy: Owner

  data:
    - secretKey: api-key
      remoteRef:
        key: /path/to/the/secret/api-key
    - secretKey: db-password
      remoteRef:
        key: /path/to/the/secret/db-password
</code></pre></div></div>
<ul>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">refreshInterval</code>: How often ESO refreshes values from Akeyless.</li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">secretStoreRef</code>: Which <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">SecretStore</code> or <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ClusterSecretStore</code> to use.</li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">target.name</code>: Name of the Kubernetes Secret created.</li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">data[*].secretKey</code>: Key name inside the Kubernetes Secret.</li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">data[*].remoteRef.key</code>: Full path of the item in Akeyless.</li>
</ul>
<p>Retrieve values:</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">Shell</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-shell theme-light" data-lang="shell" name="" tabindex="0">kubectl get secret app-config-secret -n akeyless-demo -o jsonpath=&#x27;{.data.api-key}&#x27; | base64 -d
</code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="using-datafrom-to-extract-json"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-using-data-from-to-extract-json" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Using <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">dataFrom</code> to Extract JSON</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Using " class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#using-datafrom-to-extract-json"></a></h3>
<p>If an Akeyless secret contains JSON, <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">dataFrom.extract</code> can be used to split that JSON into multiple keys in the Kubernetes Secret.</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">apiVersion: external-secrets.io/v1
kind: ExternalSecret
metadata:
  name: akeyless-external-secret-json
  namespace: akeyless-demo
spec:
  refreshInterval: 1h

  secretStoreRef:
    kind: SecretStore
    name: akeyless-secret-store

  target:
    name: app-config-json
    creationPolicy: Owner

  dataFrom:
    - extract:
        key: /path/to/the/json-secret
</code></pre></div></div>
<p>If the JSON value in Akeyless is:</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">JSON</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-json theme-light" data-lang="json" name="" tabindex="0">{
  &quot;username&quot;: &quot;demo&quot;,
  &quot;password&quot;: &quot;s3cr3t&quot;
}
</code></pre></div></div>
<p>Then the resulting Kubernetes Secret <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">app-config-json</code> will contain two keys: <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">username</code> and <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">password</code>.</p>
<p>To inspect all keys:</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">Shell</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-shell theme-light" data-lang="shell" name="" tabindex="0">kubectl get secret app-config-json -o jsonpath=&#x27;{.data}&#x27;
</code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="certificates-splitting-certificate-and-private-key"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-certificates-splitting-certificate-and-private-key" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Certificates: Splitting Certificate and Private Key</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Certificates: Splitting Certificate and Private Key" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#certificates-splitting-certificate-and-private-key"></a></h3>
<p>Akeyless certificate items typically contain separate PEM blocks for the certificate and private key. They can be mapped to <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">tls.crt</code> and <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">tls.key</code> in a Kubernetes TLS Secret.</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">apiVersion: external-secrets.io/v1
kind: ExternalSecret
metadata:
  name: akeyless-tls-secret
  namespace: akeyless-demo
spec:
  refreshInterval: 1h

  secretStoreRef:
    kind: SecretStore
    name: akeyless-secret-store

  target:
    name: my-tls-secret
    creationPolicy: Owner
    template:
      type: kubernetes.io/tls

  data:
    - secretKey: tls.crt
      remoteRef:
        key: /path/to/the/certificate-item
        property: certificate_pem

    - secretKey: tls.key
      remoteRef:
        key: /path/to/the/certificate-item
        property: private_key_pem
</code></pre></div></div>
<p>Now <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">my-tls-secret</code> can be used with a Kubernetes <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">Ingress</code> or other resource expecting a TLS Secret.</p>
<hr/>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="pushsecret-push-kubernetes-secrets-into-akeyless"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-push-secret-push-kubernetes-secrets-into-akeyless" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">PushSecret</code>: Push Kubernetes Secrets Into Akeyless</div><a aria-label="Skip link to [object Object]" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#pushsecret-push-kubernetes-secrets-into-akeyless"></a></h2>
<p><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">PushSecret</code> is used to <strong>push</strong> local Kubernetes Secrets into Akeyless, enabling a GitOps-friendly workflow where Kubernetes becomes the source of truth for some secrets.</p>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="create-a-local-kubernetes-secret"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-create-a-local-kubernetes-secret" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Create a Local Kubernetes Secret</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Create a Local Kubernetes Secret" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#create-a-local-kubernetes-secret"></a></h3>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">Shell</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-shell theme-light" data-lang="shell" name="" tabindex="0">kubectl create secret generic --from-literal=cache-pass=mypassword k8s-created-secret -n akeyless-demo
</code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="define-the-pushsecret-resource"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-define-the-push-secret-resource" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Define the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">PushSecret</code> Resource</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Define the " class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#define-the-pushsecret-resource"></a></h3>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">apiVersion: external-secrets.io/v1alpha1
kind: PushSecret
metadata:
  name: push-secret
  namespace: akeyless-demo
spec:
  refreshInterval: 5s
  updatePolicy: Replace
  deletionPolicy: Delete

  secretStoreRefs:
    - name: akeyless-secret-store
      kind: SecretStore

  selector:
    secret:
      name: k8s-created-secret

  data:
    - match:
        remoteRef:
          remoteKey: eso-created/my-secret
</code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="heading heading-4 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="key-fields-1"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-key-fields" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Key Fields</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Key Fields" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#key-fields-1"></a></h4>
<ul>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">refreshInterval</code>: How often ESO checks for changes in the Kubernetes Secret.</li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">updatePolicy</code>: Whether to replace or merge when updating the provider secret.</li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">deletionPolicy</code>: Whether to delete the provider secret when the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">PushSecret</code> resource is deleted.</li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">remoteKey</code>: Path where the secret will be stored in Akeyless.</li>
</ul>
<p>Applying this manifest will create an Akeyless secret named <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">eso-created/my-secret</code> whose value is derived from <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">k8s-created-secret</code> (for example <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">{&quot;cache-pass&quot;:&quot;mypassword&quot;}</code>).</p>
<hr/>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="azure-ad-managed-identity-sub-claim-example"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-azure-ad-managed-identity-sub-claim-example" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Azure AD Managed Identity: Sub-Claim Example</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Azure AD Managed Identity: Sub-Claim Example" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#azure-ad-managed-identity-sub-claim-example"></a></h2>
<p>This section illustrates how to use <strong>Azure AD Managed Identity</strong> on AKS in combination with an Akeyless <strong>Azure AD Authentication Method</strong> that enforces <strong>sub-claims</strong>, such as <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">xms_mirid</code> (Managed Identity resource ID) and <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">oid</code> (user/object ID).</p>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="example-akeyless-azure-ad-auth-method-with-sub-claims"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-example-akeyless-azure-ad-auth-method-with-sub-claims" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Example: Akeyless Azure AD Auth Method With Sub-Claims</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Example: Akeyless Azure AD Auth Method With Sub-Claims" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#example-akeyless-azure-ad-auth-method-with-sub-claims"></a></h3>
<p>Below is a truncated example of an Azure AD Auth Method with <strong>role associations</strong> and <strong>sub-claims</strong> that bind the role to specific identities:</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">JSON</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-json theme-light" data-lang="json" name="" tabindex="0">{
  &quot;name&quot;: &quot;devops/azure/akeyless-azure-ad-auth&quot;,
  &quot;auth_method_access_id&quot;: &quot;p-xxxxx&quot;,
  &quot;access_info&quot;: {
    &quot;rules_type&quot;: &quot;azure_ad&quot;,
    &quot;force_sub_claims&quot;: true,
    &quot;azure_ad_access_rules&quot;: {
      &quot;issuer&quot;: &quot;https://sts.windows.net/&lt;tenant-id&gt;/&quot;,
      &quot;jwks_uri&quot;: &quot;https://login.microsoftonline.com/common/discovery/keys&quot;,
      &quot;bound_tenant_id&quot;: &quot;&lt;tenant-id&gt;&quot;
    }
  },
  &quot;auth_method_roles_assoc&quot;: [
    {
      &quot;role_name&quot;: &quot;devops/devops-api-role&quot;,
      &quot;auth_method_sub_claims&quot;: {
        &quot;xms_mirid&quot;: [
          &quot;/subscriptions/.../resourcegroups/.../providers/Microsoft.ManagedIdentity/userAssignedIdentities/identities&quot;
        ]
      }
    },
    {
      &quot;role_name&quot;: &quot;devops/devops-api-role&quot;,
      &quot;auth_method_sub_claims&quot;: {
        &quot;oid&quot;: [
          &quot;11108008-9999-abcd-1234-ab123456abc1&quot;
        ]
      }
    },
    {
      &quot;role_name&quot;: &quot;devops/devops-api-role&quot;,
      &quot;auth_method_sub_claims&quot;: {
        &quot;xms_mirid&quot;: [
          &quot;/subscriptions/.../userAssignedIdentities/UserAkeylessGWManagedID&quot;,
          &quot;/subscriptions/.../userAssignedIdentities/identities&quot;
        ]
      }
    }
  ]
}
</code></pre></div></div>
<p>In this configuration:</p>
<ul>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">force_sub_claims: true</code> requires that <strong>at least one sub-claim match</strong> for access to be granted.</li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">auth_method_sub_claims.xms_mirid</code> binds access to specific <strong>user-assigned Managed Identities</strong>.</li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">auth_method_sub_claims.oid</code> can bind access to specific Azure AD identities (for example, human users or service principals).</li>
</ul>
<p>The associated role <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">devops/devops-api-role</code> typically grants <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">read</code>, <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">list</code>, <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">create</code>, <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">update</code>, and <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">delete</code> capabilities on paths such as <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">/devops/</code> and <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">/SPIRE/</code>.</p>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="kubernetes-manifests-for-eso-using-azure-ad-auth"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-kubernetes-manifests-for-eso-using-azure-ad-auth" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Kubernetes Manifests for ESO Using Azure AD Auth</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Kubernetes Manifests for ESO Using Azure AD Auth" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#kubernetes-manifests-for-eso-using-azure-ad-auth"></a></h3>
<p>The following manifests show how to use the above Auth Method from an AKS cluster with ESO.</p>
<h4 class="heading heading-4 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="credentials-secret-azure-ad"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-credentials-secret-azure-ad" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Credentials Secret (Azure AD)</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Credentials Secret (Azure AD)" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#credentials-secret-azure-ad"></a></h4>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">apiVersion: v1
kind: Secret
metadata:
  name: akeyless-azure-creds
  namespace: app-test
type: Opaque
stringData:
  accessId: &quot;p-xxxxx&quot;
  accessType: &quot;azure_ad&quot; # Use Azure AD Auth Method
  accessTypeParam: &quot;&quot;      # Required field; can be empty when binding by way of sub-claims
</code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="heading heading-4 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="secretstore-referencing-the-azure-ad-credentials"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-secret-store-referencing-the-azure-ad-credentials" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>SecretStore Referencing the Azure AD Credentials</div><a aria-label="Skip link to SecretStore Referencing the Azure AD Credentials" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#secretstore-referencing-the-azure-ad-credentials"></a></h4>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">apiVersion: external-secrets.io/v1
kind: SecretStore
metadata:
  name: akeyless-store
  namespace: app-test
spec:
  provider:
    akeyless:
      akeylessGWApiURL: &quot;https://api.akeyless.io&quot;
      # Optional: use a specific ServiceAccount for ESO controller in this namespace
      serviceAccountRef:
        name: app-test
      authSecretRef:
        secretRef:
          accessID:
            name: akeyless-azure-creds
            key: accessId
          accessType:
            name: akeyless-azure-creds
            key: accessType
          accessTypeParam:
            name: akeyless-azure-creds
            key: accessTypeParam
</code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="heading heading-4 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="externalsecret-consuming-a-secret-by-way-of-the-secretstore"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-external-secret-consuming-a-secret-by-way-of-the-secret-store" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>ExternalSecret Consuming a Secret by way of the SecretStore</div><a aria-label="Skip link to ExternalSecret Consuming a Secret by way of the SecretStore" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#externalsecret-consuming-a-secret-by-way-of-the-secretstore"></a></h4>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">YAML</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-yaml theme-light" data-lang="yaml" name="" tabindex="0">apiVersion: external-secrets.io/v1
kind: ExternalSecret
metadata:
  name: app-api-secret
  namespace: app-test
spec:
  refreshInterval: 1h
  secretStoreRef:
    name: akeyless-store
    kind: SecretStore
  target:
    name: app-api-secret
    creationPolicy: Owner
  data:
    - secretKey: api-key
      remoteRef:
        key: /devops/static_secret_1
</code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="heading heading-4 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="retrieving-the-synced-secret"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-retrieving-the-synced-secret" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Retrieving the Synced Secret</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Retrieving the Synced Secret" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#retrieving-the-synced-secret"></a></h4>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">Shell</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-shell theme-light" data-lang="shell" name="" tabindex="0">kubectl -n app-test get secret app-api-secret -o jsonpath=&quot;{.data.api-key}&quot; | base64 -d
</code></pre></div></div>
<p>This pattern ties together:</p>
<ul>
<li>AKS nodes or workloads using <strong>Managed Identity</strong>,</li>
<li>An Akeyless <strong>Azure AD Auth Method</strong> with sub-claim constraints, and</li>
<li>ESO as the consumer that syncs secrets into Kubernetes.</li>
</ul>
<hr/>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="tutorial"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-tutorial" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Tutorial</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Tutorial" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#tutorial"></a></h2>

Operator","type":"basic","updated_at":"2026-03-10T11:54:58.000Z","uri":"/branches/1.0/guides/external-secrets-operator","appearance":{"icon":{"name":null,"type":null}},"category":{"uri":"/branches/1.0/categories/guides/Integrations
